\isatagdocument
%
\isamarkupsubsection{The complete divisibility lattice on \isa{nat} and \isa{int}%
}
\isamarkuptrue%
%
\endisatagdocument
{\isafolddocument}%
%
\isadelimdocument
%
\endisadelimdocument
%
\begin{isamarkuptext}%
Lifting \isa{gcd} and \isa{lcm} to sets (\isa{Gcd} / \isa{Lcm}).
  \isa{Gcd} is defined via \isa{Lcm} to facilitate the proof that we have a complete lattice.%
\end{isamarkuptext}\isamarkuptrue%
\isacommand{instantiation}\isamarkupfalse%
\ nat\ {\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}\ semiring{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}Gcd\isanewline
\isakeyword{begin}\isanewline
\isanewline
\isacommand{interpretation}\isamarkupfalse%
\ semilattice{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}neutr{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}set\ lcm\ {\isachardoublequoteopen}{\isadigit{1}}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}{\isacharcolon}{\kern0pt}nat{\isachardoublequoteclose}\isanewline
%
\isadelimproof
\ \ %
\endisadelimproof
%
\isatagproof
\isacommand{by}\isamarkupfalse%
\ standard\ simp{\isacharunderscore}{\kern0pt}all%
\endisatagproof
{\isafoldproof}%
%
\isadelimproof
\isanewline
%
\endisadelimproof
\isanewline

\isanewline
